81173f92a3e262039deeb31a9cce9995e27a5246|2017-10-20|Peter Koval|some troubles solved, only a small change in 0041 remains to understand. The nao branch will be later rewritten to comply pySCF more closely. The system of classes would be nao (similar to mole) -> scf (similar to scf) -> tddft_iter (similar to tddft). During the initializaion of scf, I want to inherit from nao and add product basis to the scf class (but without computing the kernel). During the initialization of tddft_iter, I want to inherit from scf and initialize the kernel. Doing in this way, the class scf will be prepared for an SCF, GW or TDDFT with nao. The initialization from the siesta output should be done then for the class scf. The class scf will be similar to the type system_vars_t in Fortran.
